<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нарушить.html>нару́шить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">narúšitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нарушать.html>наруша́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">narušátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нарушить.html>нару́шить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to violate, to break
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нарушать.html>наруша́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:закон.html>зако́н</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>narušátʹ</b> zakón</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>to break</b> the law</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нарушать.html>наруша́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:правило.html>пра́вило</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>narušátʹ</b> právilo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to violate/break the/a rule, depart from a rule</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нарушать.html>наруша́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>narušátʹ</b> slóvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to break one's word, to go back upon / on one's word (breaking promise or contract)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нарушать.html>наруша́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:порядок.html>поря́док</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>narušátʹ</b> porjádok</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to break the order</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нарушать.html>наруша́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:право.html>права́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́ка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>narušátʹ</b> pravá čelovéka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to violate human rights</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нарушать.html>наруша́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:государственный.html>госуда́рственную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:граница.html>грани́цу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>narušátʹ</b> gosudárstvennuju granícu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to violate the state border</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to upset, to disrupt
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нарушать.html>наруша́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:равновесие.html>равнове́сие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́л</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>narušátʹ</b> ravnovésije sil</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to upset the balance of power</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нарушать.html>наруша́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:покой.html>поко́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>narušátʹ</b> pokój</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to shatter peace and quiet (of)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нарушать.html>наруша́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:молчание.html>молча́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>narušátʹ</b> molčánije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to break the silence</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нарушаться.html>наруша́ться</a> (10423)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ру<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ша́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:нарушиться.html>нару́шиться</a>.

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рушить.html>ру́шить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rúšitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нарушить.html>нару́шить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">narúšitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нарушать.html>наруша́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to violate, to break

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нарушить.html>нару́шить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:правило.html>пра́вило</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>narúšitʹ</b> právilo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to violate/break the/a rule, depart from a rule</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нарушить.html>нару́шить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>narúšitʹ</b> slóvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to break one's word, to go back upon / on one's word (breaking promise or contract)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нарушить.html>нару́шить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:порядок.html>поря́док</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>narúšitʹ</b> porjádok</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to break the order</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нарушить.html>нару́шить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:право.html>права́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́ка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>narúšitʹ</b> pravá čelovéka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to violate human rights</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нарушить.html>нару́шить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:государственный.html>госуда́рственную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:граница.html>грани́цу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>narúšitʹ</b> gosudárstvennuju granícu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to violate the state border</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to upset, to disrupt
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нарушить.html>нару́шить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:равновесие.html>равнове́сие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́л</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>narúšitʹ</b> ravnovésije sil</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to upset the balance of power</span></div></dd>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нарушить.html>нару́шить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:молчание.html>молча́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>narúšitʹ</b> molčánije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to break the silence</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нарушиться.html>нару́шиться</a></b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нары.html>на́ры</a> (3474)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нары.html>на́ры</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">náry</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нары.html>на́р</a></b>, <i>plural only</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>plank bed <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">often used in prisons</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, bunk</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">idiomatic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> prison, jail
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>На</a> кана́рах — лу́чше, <a href = vnd.unilang:чем.html>чем</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нары.html>на́рах</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Na Kanárax — lúčše, čem na <b>nárax</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">On the Canary Islands is better than on the (prison) <b>bunk</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нары.html>на́ры</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">náry</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">nominative plural of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нары.html>на́р</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nar</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нарываться.html>нарыва́ться</a> (25937)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">нарыва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">naryvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нарываться.html>нарыва́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">naryvátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нарваться.html>нарва́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to run <i>(into)</i>, to run up <i>(on, against)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нарываться.html>нарыва́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:неприятность.html>неприя́тность</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>naryvátʹsja</b> na neprijátnostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to run into trouble</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to ask <i>(for)</i>, to invite
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ты</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нарываться.html>нарыва́ешься</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:грубость.html>гру́бость</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ty <b>naryváješʹsja</b> na grúbostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">one can't help being rude with you</span></div></dd></dl></li>

***нарядить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нарядить.html>наряди́ть</a> (20482)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рядить.html>ряди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rjadítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нарядить.html>наряди́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">narjadítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">наряжа́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to dress up, to dress out, to apparel <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to dress or clothe</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to adorn, to decorate</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нарядить.html>наряди́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">narjadítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">наряжа́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to dispatch (someone) on an assignment</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to establish, to organize (e.g. an investigation)</li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нарядить.html>наряди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">narjadítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нарядиться.html>наряди́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">narjadítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наряжаться.html>наряжа́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to dress smartly</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to dress improperly or inappropriately</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to dress as, to dress in imitation of <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ instrumental, someone</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нарядить.html>наряди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">narjadítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наряд.html>наря́д</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">narjád</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нарядный.html>наря́дный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">narjádnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)наря́днее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)наря́дней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>well-dressed (of a person)</li>
<li>smart, natty, spiffy (of clothes)</li></ol>

***наряжаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наряжаться.html>наряжа́ться</a> (28962)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">наряжа́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">narjažátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наряжаться.html>наряжа́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">narjažátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нарядиться.html>наряди́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to dress smartly</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to dress improperly or inappropriately</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to dress as, to dress in imitation of <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ instrumental, someone</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:садить.html>сади́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sadítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насадить.html>насади́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nasadítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насаживать.html>наса́живать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to get <i>(on)</i>, to haft <i>(on)</i>, to stick, to pin, to spit</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насадить.html>насади́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nasadítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насаждать.html>насажда́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to spread, to implant, to instill, to ingraft</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:насадка.html>наса́дка</a> (31266)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насадить.html>насади́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nasadítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насадка.html>наса́дка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nasádka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насадка.html>наса́дки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насадка.html>наса́дки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насадка.html>наса́док</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>nozzle, mouthpiece</li>
<li>setting, putting on (action)</li>
<li>(fishing) bait</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>сви́с<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ты</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>вать</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — насвистать, насвистеть.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>на-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-свист-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ыва</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
